    // Dapatkan user-agent browser/app
    const ua = navigator.userAgent;

    // Senarai yang dibenarkan (boleh tambah jika mahu)
    const allowedAgents = [
      'OTTPlayer',
      'OTT Navigator',
      'TiviMate',
      'Perfect Player',
      'Smart IPTV',
      'IPTV'
    ];

    // Semak sama ada dibenarkan
    let allowed = false;
    for (let i = 0; i < allowedAgents.length; i++) {
      if (ua.includes(allowedAgents[i])) {
        allowed = true;
        break;
      }
    }

    // Jika tak dibenarkan, redirect ke laman larangan
    if (!allowed) {
      window.location.href = "http://bozzku.xyz/limit.html";
    }
  </script>
